181|205058|              let regex = buildRegex()

201|8c8340|                    withTemplate: replaceQuery

206|4e2d32|                }

208|adc83b|

260|4e4994|    private func executeSearch() -> [SearchResult] {
261|808213|        guard let core = editorCore else { return [] }
262|06469e|        guard let regex = buildRegex() else { return [] }
263|adc83b|
264|b128e6|        struct Target {
265|d0d64f|            let url: URL?
266|649854|            let filePath: String
267|062bcc|            let fileName: String
268|6ffdc2|            let content: String
269|5f3077|        }
270|adc83b|
271|422382|        let targets: [Target] = {
272|450a38|            switch searchScope {
273|08df20|            case .currentFile:
274|c935e6|                guard let tab = core.activeTab else { return [] }
275|666545|                let path = tab.url?.path ?? tab.fileName
276|57a63d|                return [Target(url: tab.url, filePath: path, fileName: tab.fileName, content: tab.content)]
277|adc83b|
278|231fff|            case .openFiles:
279|09a4e8|                return core.tabs.map { tab in
280|66779a|                    let path = tab.url?.path ?? tab.fileName
281|be9fba|                    return Target(url: tab.url, filePath: path, fileName: tab.fileName, content: tab.content)
282|4e2d32|                }
283|adc83b|
284|2fb721|            case .workspace:
285|481d56|                guard let tree = core.fileNavigator?.fileTree else { return [] }
286|3d2cac|                let urls = collectFileURLs(from: tree)
287|c4e083|                return urls.compactMap { url in
288|e86233|                    guard let content = try? String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8) else { return nil }
289|3223da|                    return Target(url: url, filePath: url.path, fileName: url.lastPathComponent, content: content)
290|4e2d32|                }
291|a7dc16|            }
292|41cc2d|        }()
293|adc83b|
294|ede8fe|        var results: [SearchResult] = []
295|87d422|        results.reserveCapacity(64)
296|adc83b|
297|7e02cf|        for target in targets {
298|e64b6f|            let text = target.content
299|922eef|            let nsText = text as NSString
300|adc83b|
301|a53603|            let searchRange: NSRange
302|c50c1e|            if searchInSelection,
303|e6cc02|               searchScope == .currentFile,
304|9b8ef5|               let selection = core.currentSelectionRange {
305|92f918|                searchRange = selection
306|f5a6eb|            } else {
307|fd803f|                searchRange = NSRange(location: 0, length: nsText.length)
308|a7dc16|            }
309|adc83b|
310|5842db|            let matches = regex.matches(in: text, options: [], range: searchRange)
311|7c58fe|            for match in matches {
312|ed8ef0|                let r = match.range
313|30dcc2|                guard let swiftRange = Range(r, in: text) else { continue }
314|adc83b|
315|9f4e6b|                // 1-based line number
316|854f7d|                let prefix = nsText.substring(to: min(r.location, nsText.length))
317|caf675|                let lineNumber = prefix.components(separatedBy: "\n").count
318|adc83b|
319|7f7e0b|                // Full line content
320|bab0af|                let lineRange = nsText.lineRange(for: r)
321|b88e01|                var lineContent = nsText.substring(with: lineRange)
322|0bfc40|                lineContent = lineContent.trimmingCharacters(in: .newlines)
323|adc83b|
324|944744|                results.append(
325|5c7081|                    SearchResult(
326|d50448|                        filePath: target.filePath,
327|ab39a1|                        fileName: target.fileName,
328|36535d|                        url: target.url,
329|3d467c|                        lineNumber: lineNumber,
330|e9c207|                        lineContent: lineContent,
331|817f47|                        matchRange: swiftRange,
332|bd73c0|                        matchNSRange: r,
333|c65676|                        contextBefore: nil,
334|9ce3a8|                        contextAfter: nil
335|1961a4|                    )
336|6f642e|                )
337|a7dc16|            }
338|5f3077|        }
339|adc83b|
340|32b4af|        return results
341|27e597|    }

343|49f5dd|    private func buildRegex() -> NSRegularExpression? {
344|aa8b8c|        guard !searchQuery.isEmpty else { return nil }
345|adc83b|
346|d13bab|        let pattern: String
347|2c0ffc|        if useRegex {
348|ee8ad7|            pattern = searchQuery
349|b31999|        } else {
350|99a63d|            pattern = NSRegularExpression.escapedPattern(for: searchQuery)
351|5f3077|        }
352|adc83b|

354|d256d8|        let options: NSRegularExpression.Options = isCaseSensitive ? [] : [.caseInsensitive]
355|adc83b|

357|27e597|    }

152|b724e3|    /// Insert text at all cursor positions
153|f215f3|    func insertText(_ text: String, in fullText: inout String) {
154|7af105|        // Process from start -> end while tracking how prior edits shift later cursor positions.
155|4dfc73|        let sortedCursors = cursors.sorted { $0.position < $1.position }
156|b4bd74|        var delta = 0
157|adc83b|
158|7e0829|        for cursor in sortedCursors {
159|6f5089|            guard let cursorIndex = cursors.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == cursor.id }) else { continue }
160|adc83b|
161|94aef6|            if let selectionRange = cursor.selectionRange {
162|240234|                let effectiveLocation = selectionRange.location + delta
163|33054a|                let effectiveRange = NSRange(location: effectiveLocation, length: selectionRange.length)
164|adc83b|
165|6c5a92|                guard let swiftRange = Range(effectiveRange, in: fullText) else { continue }
166|adc83b|
167|5e54f3|                fullText.replaceSubrange(swiftRange, with: text)
168|adc83b|
169|9ad989|                // Cursor ends after inserted text; selection cleared.
170|1cc5b7|                cursors[cursorIndex].position = effectiveLocation + text.count
171|c0748c|                cursors[cursorIndex].anchor = nil
172|adc83b|
173|27a6d2|                delta += (text.count - selectionRange.length)
174|f5a6eb|            } else {
175|2a24c0|                let effectivePosition = cursor.position + delta
176|4ce229|                let clamped = min(max(0, effectivePosition), fullText.count)
177|660e91|                let stringIndex = fullText.index(fullText.startIndex, offsetBy: clamped)
178|adc83b|
179|0958ea|                fullText.insert(contentsOf: text, at: stringIndex)
180|adc83b|
181|9b2357|                cursors[cursorIndex].position = clamped + text.count
182|1198fc|                delta += text.count
183|a7dc16|            }
184|5f3077|        }
185|adc83b|
186|4120e8|        // Keep state sane if multiple edits collapse cursors onto the same location.
187|55724c|        removeDuplicateCursors()
188|27e597|    }
189|b4687f|

193|b4bd74|        var delta = 0
194|adc83b|

250|63c94d|    func findAllOccurrences(of searchString: String, caseSensitive: Bool = true) -> [NSRange] {
251|35cdd0|        var ranges: [NSRange] = []
252|78712f|        var searchRange = startIndex..<endIndex
253|e443de|        let options: String.CompareOptions = caseSensitive ? [] : .caseInsensitive
254|d6ed84|

259|5f3077|        }

266|e6a5fe|        guard position < count else { return nil }

269|d6ed84|

273|5f3077|        }

50|b298bb|    // Helper for Hex Colors
51|8792bd|    static func hex(_ hex: String) -> Color {
52|a7cf95|        var hexSanitized = hex.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
53|47dd68|        hexSanitized = hexSanitized.replacingOccurrences(of: "#", with: "")
54|d6ed84|        
55|d3af08|        var rgb: UInt64 = 0
56|f1bde0|        Scanner(string: hexSanitized).scanHexInt64(&rgb)
57|d6ed84|        
58|61c152|        let r = Double((rgb & 0xFF0000) >> 16) / 255.0
59|c6183b|        let g = Double((rgb & 0x00FF00) >> 8) / 255.0
60|3cf70f|        let b = Double(rgb & 0x0000FF) / 255.0
61|d6ed84|        
62|8616b6|        return Color(red: r, green: g, blue: b)
63|27e597|    }
64|b4687f|

535|dd18bb|// Go Example - HTTP Server with Goroutines
536|af96a5|package main
537|adc83b|
538|f7ab87|import (
539|f48f0e|\t"context"
540|567e13|\t"encoding/json"

547|adc83b|
548|39ac9c|// User represents a user in the system
549|00db38|type User struct {
550|c77d6f|\tID        int       `json:"id"`
551|4698d5|\tName      string    `json:"name"`
552|b65b1b|\tEmail     string    `json:"email"`
553|2ed51e|\tCreatedAt time.Time `json:"created_at"`
554|b31277|}
555|adc83b|
556|e578a6|// UserStore handles user data with thread-safe access
557|c88728|type UserStore struct {
558|c3fdfb|\tmu    sync.RWMutex
559|051305|\tusers map[int]*User
560|d54867|\tnextID int
561|b31277|}
562|adc83b|
563|cc854c|func NewUserStore() *UserStore {
564|ed9ea3|\treturn &UserStore{
565|020c9f|\t\tusers:  make(map[int]*User),
566|5bfe05|\t\tnextID: 1,
567|bceb9c|\t}
568|b31277|}
569|adc83b|
570|e1b92c|func (s *UserStore) Create(name, email string) *User {
571|1db638|\ts.mu.Lock()
572|7d9ed0|\tdefer s.mu.Unlock()
573|80050b|\t
574|d8abf6|\tuser := &User{
575|e00997|\t\tID:        s.nextID,
576|6a68d6|\t\tName:      name,
577|9c5c36|\t\tEmail:     email,
578|97639d|\t\tCreatedAt: time.Now(),
579|bceb9c|\t}
580|72a210|\ts.users[user.ID] = user
581|1e16b2|\ts.nextID++
582|53ef3f|\treturn user
583|b31277|}
584|adc83b|
585|366ce6|func (s *UserStore) Get(id int) (*User, bool) {
586|4ddb51|\ts.mu.RLock()
587|bced95|\tdefer s.mu.RUnlock()
588|4eba9b|\tuser, ok := s.users[id]
589|00df77|\treturn user, ok
590|b31277|}
591|adc83b|
592|ff8f91|func handleUsers(store *UserStore) http.HandlerFunc {
593|339c11|\treturn func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
594|53b88a|\t\tswitch r.Method {
595|9d2118|\t\tcase http.MethodGet:
596|394019|\t\t\t// Return all users
597|9e9af3|\t\t\tw.Header().Set("Content-Type", "application/json")
598|43bf24|\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(store.users)
599|59888b|\t\tcase http.MethodPost:
600|0965d8|\t\t\t// Create new user
601|e913f0|\t\t\tvar req struct {
602|2f0bda|\t\t\t\tName  string `json:"name"`
603|0c4cc3|\t\t\t\tEmail string `json:"email"`
604|1f4a90|\t\t\t}
605|2b3653|\t\t\tif err := json.NewDecoder(r.Body).Decode(&req); err != nil {
606|447a17|\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusBadRequest)
607|1b1356|\t\t\t\treturn
608|1f4a90|\t\t\t}
609|b82a43|\t\t\tuser := store.Create(req.Name, req.Email)
610|d73497|\t\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusCreated)
611|17b111|\t\t\tjson.NewEncoder(w).Encode(user)
612|04883b|\t\tdefault:
613|2ea09d|\t\t\thttp.Error(w, "Method not allowed", http.StatusMethodNotAllowed)
614|53a2fc|\t\t}
615|bceb9c|\t}
616|b31277|}
617|adc83b|
618|a4072f|func main() {
619|ca7100|\tstore := NewUserStore()
620|80050b|\t
621|1b6d3b|\t// Seed some data
622|6ea9c7|\tstore.Create("Alice", "alice@example.com")
623|2c81f1|\tstore.Create("Bob", "bob@example.com")
624|80050b|\t
625|45645c|\tmux := http.NewServeMux()
626|b3170f|\tmux.HandleFunc("/api/users", handleUsers(store))
627|80050b|\t
628|a3c17c|\tserver := &http.Server{
629|879a10|\t\tAddr:         ":8080",
630|876c57|\t\tHandler:      mux,
631|a8bd2e|\t\tReadTimeout:  10 * time.Second,
632|aa51e5|\t\tWriteTimeout: 10 * time.Second,
633|bceb9c|\t}
634|80050b|\t
635|8d2b91|\tfmt.Println("Server starting on :8080")
636|fd5ced|\tlog.Fatal(server.ListenAndServe())
637|b31277|}

643|f0955b|        examples.append(Tab(
644|f13142|            fileName: "main.rs",
645|7a029b|            content: """
646|0e41ca|//! Rust Example - Async Web Server
647|fa16f5|//! Demonstrates ownership, traits, async/await, and error handling
648|adc83b|
649|9acfeb|use std::collections::HashMap;
650|b948b2|use std::sync::Arc;
651|859d9d|use tokio::sync::RwLock;
652|adc83b|
653|5f279c|/// Represents a task in our system
654|fc0948|#[derive(Debug, Clone, serde::Serialize, serde::Deserialize)]
655|9fa61b|pub struct Task {
656|eb40d9|    pub id: u64,
657|b30539|    pub title: String,
658|968947|    pub completed: bool,
659|3f7fee|    #[serde(skip_serializing_if = "Option::is_none")]
660|eb696e|    pub description: Option<String>,
661|b31277|}
662|adc83b|
663|c65acf|/// Task store with thread-safe access
664|aa97ce|pub struct TaskStore {
665|f700f3|    tasks: RwLock<HashMap<u64, Task>>,
666|4ca795|    next_id: RwLock<u64>,
667|b31277|}
668|adc83b|
669|302a3c|impl TaskStore {
670|8ad9f1|    pub fn new() -> Self {
671|3f21ea|        Self {
672|c4b209|            tasks: RwLock::new(HashMap::new()),
673|a066e2|            next_id: RwLock::new(1),
674|5f3077|        }
675|27e597|    }
676|b4687f|    
677|5b894d|    pub async fn create(&self, title: String, description: Option<String>) -> Task {
678|c96765|        let mut next_id = self.next_id.write().await;
679|582717|        let id = *next_id;
680|35ab64|        *next_id += 1;
681|d6ed84|        
682|8ffd70|        let task = Task {
683|c48bb6|            id,
684|9643f5|            title,
685|49769d|            completed: false,
686|d6d80b|            description,
687|105ee3|        };
688|d6ed84|        
689|c79c9c|        self.tasks.write().await.insert(id, task.clone());
690|9cec82|        task
691|27e597|    }
692|b4687f|    
693|d18a8f|    pub async fn get(&self, id: u64) -> Option<Task> {
694|ee96f9|        self.tasks.read().await.get(&id).cloned()
695|27e597|    }
696|b4687f|    
697|c542c4|    pub async fn list(&self) -> Vec<Task> {
698|26bc2e|        self.tasks.read().await.values().cloned().collect()
699|27e597|    }
700|b4687f|    
701|1e6608|    pub async fn complete(&self, id: u64) -> Result<Task, &'static str> {
702|8b2ab5|        let mut tasks = self.tasks.write().await;
703|1e8e13|        match tasks.get_mut(&id) {
704|7711a1|            Some(task) => {
705|9cb7d9|                task.completed = true;
706|b1925e|                Ok(task.clone())
707|a7dc16|            }
708|ba0906|            None => Err("Task not found"),
709|5f3077|        }
710|27e597|    }
711|b31277|}
712|adc83b|
713|167169|/// Error type for our application
714|351e30|#[derive(Debug, thiserror::Error)]
715|f57677|pub enum AppError {
716|552bc0|    #[error("Task not found: {0}")]
717|953fad|    NotFound(u64),
718|50ef8b|    #[error("Invalid input: {0}")]
719|e8e806|    InvalidInput(String),
720|b31277|}
721|adc83b|
722|50ce0f|#[tokio::main]
723|c703d0|async fn main() -> Result<(), Box<dyn std::error::Error>> {
724|0ea21b|    let store = Arc::new(TaskStore::new());
725|b4687f|    
726|d1b2bd|    // Create some tasks
727|2a3a42|    let task1 = store.create("Learn Rust".into(), Some("Study ownership".into())).await;
728|edbb66|    let task2 = store.create("Build app".into(), None).await;
729|b4687f|    
730|aafcec|    println!("Created tasks:");
731|9c5f1e|    for task in store.list().await {
732|2d361b|        println!("  - {} ({})", task.title, if task.completed { "✓" } else { "○" });
733|27e597|    }
734|b4687f|    
735|c1ed84|    // Complete a task
736|2d32bb|    store.complete(task1.id).await?;
737|3db4e3|    println!("\\nCompleted task: {}", task1.title);
738|b4687f|    
739|b54f61|    Ok(())
740|b31277|}

760|adc83b|
761|4dde5e|    // MARK: - Tab Management
762|adc83b|
763|76ae59|    func addTab(fileName: String = "Untitled.swift", content: String = "", url: URL? = nil) {
764|741280|        // Check if file is already open by URL
765|0ac880|        if let url = url, let existingTab = tabs.first(where: { $0.url == url }) {
766|552ca0|            activeTabId = existingTab.id
767|bef5d6|            return
768|5f3077|        }
769|d6ed84|        
770|95bffd|        // For tabs without URLs (demo/untitled), check by fileName to avoid duplicates
771|c31f65|        if url == nil, let existingTab = tabs.first(where: { $0.url == nil && $0.fileName == fileName }) {
772|552ca0|            activeTabId = existingTab.id
773|bef5d6|            return
774|5f3077|        }
775|adc83b|
776|813121|        let newTab = Tab(fileName: fileName, content: content, url: url)
777|c48936|        tabs.append(newTab)
778|731705|        activeTabId = newTab.id
779|27e597|    }
780|adc83b|
781|32d0a2|    func closeTab(id: UUID) {
782|b4daef|        guard let index = tabs.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == id }) else { return }
783|adc83b|
784|91aee8|        // Release security-scoped access if this tab was holding it.
785|f9902f|        if let url = tabs[index].url {
786|c0ad41|            releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to: url)
787|5f3077|        }
788|adc83b|
789|f8d587|        tabs.remove(at: index)
790|adc83b|
791|75e35f|        // Update active tab if we closed the active one
792|7a2997|        if activeTabId == id {
793|420e70|            if tabs.isEmpty {
794|562329|                activeTabId = nil
795|9f1ca7|            } else if index >= tabs.count {
796|fe0d6f|                activeTabId = tabs[tabs.count - 1].id
797|f5a6eb|            } else {
798|fea167|                activeTabId = tabs[index].id
799|a7dc16|            }
800|5f3077|        }
801|27e597|    }
802|adc83b|
803|da8c92|    func closeAllTabs() {
804|480aa6|        // Release security-scoped access held by any open tabs.
805|f898d5|        for tab in tabs {
806|e59f65|            if let url = tab.url {
807|4f4725|                releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to: url)
808|a7dc16|            }
809|5f3077|        }
810|adc83b|
811|11c622|        tabs.removeAll()
812|73f75a|        activeTabId = nil
813|27e597|    }
814|adc83b|
815|637501|    func closeOtherTabs(except id: UUID) {
816|7cae19|        // Release security-scoped access for tabs being closed.
817|cd7359|        for tab in tabs where tab.id != id {
818|e59f65|            if let url = tab.url {
819|4f4725|                releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to: url)
820|a7dc16|            }
821|5f3077|        }
822|adc83b|
823|9e38c3|        tabs.removeAll { $0.id != id }
824|124072|        activeTabId = id
825|27e597|    }
826|adc83b|
827|01b632|    func selectTab(id: UUID) {
828|124072|        activeTabId = id
829|27e597|    }
830|adc83b|
831|4d82c6|    func nextTab() {
832|0b2bdb|        guard let currentIndex = activeTabIndex, tabs.count > 1 else { return }
833|713593|        let nextIndex = (currentIndex + 1) % tabs.count
834|40ccb0|        activeTabId = tabs[nextIndex].id
835|27e597|    }
836|adc83b|
837|50e532|    func previousTab() {
838|0b2bdb|        guard let currentIndex = activeTabIndex, tabs.count > 1 else { return }
839|6fd10d|        let prevIndex = currentIndex == 0 ? tabs.count - 1 : currentIndex - 1
840|3edfe7|        activeTabId = tabs[prevIndex].id
841|27e597|    }
842|adc83b|
843|f5367a|    func moveTab(from source: IndexSet, to destination: Int) {
844|d4de4a|        tabs.move(fromOffsets: source, toOffset: destination)
845|27e597|    }
846|adc83b|
847|7e7abf|    // MARK: - Content Management
848|adc83b|
849|eb64ec|    func updateActiveTabContent(_ content: String) {
850|f3cca9|        guard let index = activeTabIndex else { return }
851|adc83b|
852|c5cef8|        // Avoid marking a tab dirty when we're just syncing state (e.g., initial onAppear assignment).
853|206567|        guard tabs[index].content != content else { return }
854|adc83b|
855|a364aa|        tabs[index].content = content
856|adc83b|
857|d56c61|        // Mark dirty for both saved and unsaved-new files.
858|6625d3|        tabs[index].isUnsaved = true
859|27e597|    }
860|adc83b|
861|d01c74|    func saveActiveTab() {
862|0a66d5|        guard let index = activeTabIndex,
863|b955cb|              let url = tabs[index].url else { return }
864|adc83b|
865|4da690|        do {
866|8eaea8|            if let fileNavigator {
867|30e940|                try fileNavigator.writeFile(at: url, content: tabs[index].content)
868|f5a6eb|            } else {
869|120ff8|                // Fallback: Ensure we have access when writing, even if this URL wasn't opened via openFile().
870|498601|                let didStart = (securityScopedAccessCounts[url] == nil) ? url.startAccessingSecurityScopedResource() : false
871|b9e991|                defer { if didStart { url.stopAccessingSecurityScopedResource() } }
872|6f7d16|                try tabs[index].content.write(to: url, atomically: true, encoding: .utf8)
873|a7dc16|            }
874|adc83b|
875|6adfeb|            tabs[index].isUnsaved = false
876|853889|        } catch {
877|8217f6|            print("Error saving file: \(error)")
878|5f3077|        }
879|27e597|    }
880|adc83b|
881|733624|    func saveAllTabs() {
882|be31b4|        for index in tabs.indices {
883|2205f5|            guard let url = tabs[index].url, tabs[index].isUnsaved else { continue }
884|adc83b|
885|71cc09|            do {
886|d06464|                if let fileNavigator {
887|882974|                    try fileNavigator.writeFile(at: url, content: tabs[index].content)
888|fdd0e2|                } else {
889|fa1070|                    // Fallback: Ensure we have access when writing, even if this URL wasn't opened via openFile().
890|a62986|                    let didStart = (securityScopedAccessCounts[url] == nil) ? url.startAccessingSecurityScopedResource() : false
891|981337|                    defer { if didStart { url.stopAccessingSecurityScopedResource() } }
892|5eb718|                    try tabs[index].content.write(to: url, atomically: true, encoding: .utf8)
893|4e2d32|                }
894|adc83b|
895|c47dbe|                tabs[index].isUnsaved = false
896|91b9a2|            } catch {
897|a5c86a|                print("Error saving file: \(error)")
898|a7dc16|            }
899|5f3077|        }
900|27e597|    }
901|adc83b|
902|7fcf6b|    // MARK: - File Operations
903|adc83b|
904|c94d4f|    /// Retain security scoped access for as long as a tab referencing the URL is open.
905|80f870|    /// - Returns: `true` if access was retained (either already retained or started successfully).
906|144775|    @discardableResult
907|047478|    private func retainSecurityScopedAccess(to url: URL) -> Bool {
908|3361e8|        if let count = securityScopedAccessCounts[url] {
909|74a992|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = count + 1
910|40cfc4|            return true
911|5f3077|        }
912|adc83b|
913|6bae9a|        let started = url.startAccessingSecurityScopedResource()
914|eab9dd|        if started {
915|f70ee6|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = 1
916|40cfc4|            return true
917|5f3077|        }
918|adc83b|
919|e24e9c|        // Not all URLs are security-scoped; startAccessing may legitimately return false.
920|dc1500|        return false
921|27e597|    }
922|adc83b|
923|bb512f|    private func releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to url: URL) {
924|e6f2d9|        guard let count = securityScopedAccessCounts[url] else { return }
925|d1b9b6|        if count <= 1 {
926|a8ee0e|            securityScopedAccessCounts.removeValue(forKey: url)
927|1a1387|            url.stopAccessingSecurityScopedResource()
928|b31999|        } else {
929|385b72|            securityScopedAccessCounts[url] = count - 1
930|5f3077|        }
931|27e597|    }
932|adc83b|
933|cf78ab|    func openFile(from url: URL) {
934|588853|        // If already open, just activate it (and avoid re-reading / re-requesting access).
935|b525f3|        if let existingTab = tabs.first(where: { $0.url == url }) {
936|552ca0|            activeTabId = existingTab.id
937|bef5d6|            return
938|5f3077|        }
939|adc83b|
940|932f65|        // IMPORTANT (BUG-005):
941|473a90|        // Do not early-return if startAccessingSecurityScopedResource() fails.
942|9fa2d8|        // For many URLs (non-security-scoped, or when parent scope is active), this may return false,
943|66c5ff|        // but the file is still readable. We retain access if available.
944|b64f72|        let retained = retainSecurityScopedAccess(to: url)
945|adc83b|
946|4da690|        do {
947|71b351|            let content = try String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8)
948|b7a845|            addTab(fileName: url.lastPathComponent, content: content, url: url)
949|adc83b|
950|029423|            // Index the file in Spotlight for search
951|89eebb|            SpotlightManager.shared.indexFile(url: url, content: content, fileName: url.lastPathComponent)
952|853889|        } catch {
953|6234c2|            print("Error opening file: \(error)")
954|b8e2ff|            if retained {
955|3785d1|                // We retained access but failed to open; release our retain.
956|4f4725|                releaseSecurityScopedAccess(to: url)
957|a7dc16|            }
958|5f3077|        }
959|27e597|    }
960|adc83b|
961|ecab4a|    func openFile(_ fileItem: FileItem) {
962|5644a7|        guard let url = fileItem.url else {
963|5428ce|            // Try path
964|cc691d|            if !fileItem.path.isEmpty {
965|0d25db|                let fileURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: fileItem.path)
966|04ee6d|                openFile(from: fileURL)
967|a7dc16|            }
968|bef5d6|            return
969|5f3077|        }
970|aa85ed|        openFile(from: url)
971|27e597|    }

974|adc83b|
975|9aaca8|    /// Called when a file or folder is moved/renamed in the file system.
976|fa3810|    /// Updates any open tabs that reference the old URL.
977|1aeb4b|    func handleFileSystemItemMoved(from oldURL: URL, to newURL: URL) {
978|be31b4|        for index in tabs.indices {
979|73b1a5|            guard let tabURL = tabs[index].url else { continue }
980|adc83b|
981|d91d40|            // Check if tab URL matches the moved item or is inside it (for folders)
982|6c0d3c|            let oldPath = oldURL.standardizedFileURL.path
983|354993|            let tabPath = tabURL.standardizedFileURL.path
984|adc83b|
985|ca2206|            if tabPath == oldPath {
986|5a4762|                // Direct match - update URL
987|93dccc|                tabs[index].url = newURL
988|f8a1b8|                tabs[index].fileName = newURL.lastPathComponent
989|d38dd0|            } else if tabPath.hasPrefix(oldPath + "/") {
990|cbbd97|                // Tab is inside a moved folder - update the path prefix
991|14ba8e|                let relativePath = String(tabPath.dropFirst(oldPath.count))
992|a19b0f|                let newTabURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: newURL.path + relativePath)
993|cf0bad|                tabs[index].url = newTabURL
994|a7dc16|            }
995|5f3077|        }
996|27e597|    }
997|adc83b|
998|8e6575|    /// Called when a file or folder is deleted from the file system.
999|cc8758|    /// Closes any open tabs that reference the deleted item.
1000|c5a4eb|    func handleFileSystemItemDeleted(at url: URL) {
1001|2e29c5|        let deletedPath = url.standardizedFileURL.path
1002|adc83b|
1003|1f90b1|        // Find all tabs that should be closed
1004|e5b209|        let tabsToClose = tabs.filter { tab in
1005|2a4205|            guard let tabURL = tab.url else { return false }
1006|354993|            let tabPath = tabURL.standardizedFileURL.path
1007|5f7d97|            // Close if exact match or if tab is inside deleted folder
1008|5ea75a|            return tabPath == deletedPath || tabPath.hasPrefix(deletedPath + "/")
1009|5f3077|        }
1010|adc83b|
1011|a7d718|        // Close the tabs (release security access)
1012|97cba5|        for tab in tabsToClose {
1013|cf059e|            closeTab(id: tab.id)
1014|5f3077|        }
1015|27e597|    }

1116|44d2df|    /// Add cursor on the line above (Cmd+Option+Up)
1117|2c94f4|    func addCursorAbove() {
1118|f3cca9|        guard let index = activeTabIndex else { return }
1119|760df9|        let content = tabs[index].content
1120|d6ed84|        
1121|c36153|        guard let primary = multiCursorState.primaryCursor else { return }
1122|d6ed84|        
1123|97e112|        // Find current line and column
1124|cae86c|        let lines = content.components(separatedBy: "\n")
1125|4c16f5|        var currentLine = 0
1126|788b38|        var charCount = 0
1127|efbb41|        var columnInLine = 0
1128|d6ed84|        
1129|d1a1ab|        for (lineIndex, line) in lines.enumerated() {
1130|28f01c|            let lineLength = line.count + 1 // +1 for newline
1131|855639|            if charCount + lineLength > primary.position {
1132|1f2410|                currentLine = lineIndex
1133|e165bc|                columnInLine = primary.position - charCount
1134|74cfd8|                break
1135|a7dc16|            }
1136|8f266f|            charCount += lineLength
1137|5f3077|        }
1138|d6ed84|        
1139|4ff883|        // Can't add cursor above line 0
1140|b7a259|        guard currentLine > 0 else { return }
1141|d6ed84|        
1142|ce6291|        // Calculate position on line above
1143|899b8a|        let targetLine = currentLine - 1
1144|e8b652|        var targetPosition = 0
1145|4dc12b|        for i in 0..<targetLine {
1146|8e5904|            targetPosition += lines[i].count + 1
1147|5f3077|        }
1148|90bb82|        targetPosition += min(columnInLine, lines[targetLine].count)
1149|d6ed84|        
1150|22be0f|        multiCursorState.addCursor(at: targetPosition)
1151|27e597|    }

1190|77aabc|    /// Add next occurrence of current selection (Cmd+D)
1191|e6ce2e|    func addNextOccurrence() {
1192|f3cca9|        guard let index = activeTabIndex else { return }
1193|760df9|        let content = tabs[index].content
1194|adc83b|
1195|5425d2|        // Get the word/selection to search for
1196|14ac96|        let searchText: String
1197|b70289|        let startPosition: Int
1198|adc83b|
1199|cfba87|        if let range = currentSelectionRange, range.length > 0,
1200|0939c5|           let swiftRange = Range(range, in: content) {
1201|451be1|            searchText = String(content[swiftRange])
1202|0b5fe8|            startPosition = range.location + range.length
1203|f70aa5|        } else if let primary = multiCursorState.primaryCursor {
1204|aed341|            // No selection - select the word under cursor
1205|1688ec|            let wordRange = findWordAtPosition(primary.position, in: content)
1206|8dbaff|            if let range = wordRange, range.length > 0,
1207|6998ee|               let swiftRange = Range(range, in: content) {
1208|f4b9bc|                searchText = String(content[swiftRange])
1209|d7f1fc|                startPosition = range.location + range.length
1210|adc83b|

1212|0cebd2|                multiCursorState.cursors = [Cursor(position: range.location + range.length, anchor: range.location, isPrimary: true)]
1213|70c25c|                currentSelectionRange = range
1214|311604|                currentSelection = searchText
1215|53ab34|                return
1216|f5a6eb|            } else {
1217|53ab34|                return
1218|a7dc16|            }
1219|b31999|        } else {
1220|bef5d6|            return
1221|5f3077|        }
1222|adc83b|

1224|c59f65|        if let nextRange = content.findNextOccurrence(of: searchText, after: startPosition) {
1225|372de1|            // Check if this occurrence is already selected
1226|222428|            let alreadySelected = multiCursorState.cursors.contains { cursor in

1228|173534|                    return selRange.location == nextRange.location

1231|a7dc16|            }

1234|11d39c|                multiCursorState.addCursorWithSelection(
1235|b8d907|                    position: nextRange.location + nextRange.length,
1236|4db973|                    anchor: nextRange.location
1237|6f642e|                )
1238|a7dc16|            }
1239|5f3077|        }
1240|27e597|    }

1294|4c0c23|           let index = activeTabIndex {
1295|527d1a|            let content = tabs[index].content

1303|adc83b|
1304|8984f8|    /// Find word boundaries at a given position
1305|10f43e|    func findWordAtPosition(_ position: Int, in text: String) -> NSRange? {
1306|37ae73|        guard position >= 0 && position <= text.count else { return nil }
1307|adc83b|
1308|599630|        let nsText = text as NSString
1309|026ed8|        let wordCharacters = CharacterSet.alphanumerics.union(CharacterSet(charactersIn: "_"))
1310|adc83b|
1311|b5bfb0|        // Find start of word
1312|def66a|        var start = position
1313|aaa57c|        while start > 0 {
1314|148e5a|            let char = nsText.substring(with: NSRange(location: start - 1, length: 1))
1315|70b198|            if char.unicodeScalars.allSatisfy({ wordCharacters.contains($0) }) {
1316|0c6efe|                start -= 1
1317|f5a6eb|            } else {
1318|74cfd8|                break
1319|a7dc16|            }
1320|5f3077|        }
1321|adc83b|
1322|3d8df8|        // Find end of word
1323|f5c145|        var end = position
1324|b8851f|        while end < nsText.length {
1325|244ed1|            let char = nsText.substring(with: NSRange(location: end, length: 1))
1326|70b198|            if char.unicodeScalars.allSatisfy({ wordCharacters.contains($0) }) {
1327|fddf9a|                end += 1
1328|f5a6eb|            } else {
1329|74cfd8|                break
1330|a7dc16|            }
1331|5f3077|        }
1332|adc83b|
1333|77048a|        if start == end {
1334|1c8557|            return nil
1335|5f3077|        }
1336|adc83b|
1337|469001|        return NSRange(location: start, length: end - start)
1338|27e597|    }

1344|a206bf|                resetToSingleCursor(at: primary.position)

1346|5f3077|        }
1347|27e597|    }

265|adc83b|

277|c19b31|                let children = contents.compactMap { buildFileTree(at: $0) }.sorted { $0.name < $1.name }

310|0fd45c|    @MainActor
311|b8b714|    func sendMessage(_ content: String, context: String? = nil) async {
312|915e6f|        guard hasValidAPIKey() else {
313|06856b|            error = "Please set your API key in settings"
314|bef5d6|            return
315|5f3077|        }
316|d6ed84|        
317|e352e6|        let userMessage = ChatMessage(role: .user, content: content)
318|382c05|        currentSession.messages.append(userMessage)
319|aa2963|        updateSession()
320|d6ed84|        
321|8495c1|        // Update title if first message
322|8926e1|        if currentSession.messages.count == 1 {
323|066ce6|            currentSession.title = String(content.prefix(50))
324|e749a7|            updateSession()
325|5f3077|        }
326|d6ed84|        
327|d52924|        isLoading = true
328|0406ba|        error = nil
329|dc34fb|        streamingResponse = ""
330|d6ed84|        
331|4da690|        do {
332|ce5098|            let response = try await makeAPIRequest(messages: currentSession.messages, context: context)
333|70672e|            let assistantMessage = ChatMessage(role: .assistant, content: response, codeBlocks: extractCodeBlocks(from: response))
334|c17117|            currentSession.messages.append(assistantMessage)
335|e749a7|            updateSession()
336|853889|        } catch {
337|97a9c5|            self.error = error.localizedDescription
338|5f3077|        }
339|d6ed84|        
340|295f36|        isLoading = false
341|27e597|    }

379|90c566|    private func sendAndGetResponse(_ prompt: String) async -> String {

381|1b72a2|            return "Error: Please set your API key in settings"
382|5f3077|        }

388|3b5c4f|            let messages = [ChatMessage(role: .user, content: prompt)]
389|153d92|            let response = try await makeAPIRequest(messages: messages, context: nil)
390|612c3f|            isLoading = false
391|d392d0|            return response
392|853889|        } catch {
393|612c3f|            isLoading = false
394|0cacff|            return "Error: \(error.localizedDescription)"
395|5f3077|        }
396|27e597|    }

400|0a6144|    private func makeAPIRequest(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {
401|162b99|        switch selectedProvider {
402|6ca85d|        case .openai:
403|d9a528|            return try await callOpenAI(messages: messages, context: context)
404|2b5eb0|        case .anthropic:
405|afe61a|            return try await callAnthropic(messages: messages, context: context)
406|51e5bc|        case .google:
407|688f02|            return try await callGoogle(messages: messages, context: context)
408|a90b5c|        case .kimi:
409|467f79|            return try await callKimi(messages: messages, context: context)
410|448974|        case .glm:
411|d03556|            return try await callGLM(messages: messages, context: context)
412|6a2402|        case .groq:
413|2fdc7f|            return try await callGroq(messages: messages, context: context)
414|586fca|        case .deepseek:
415|b7290a|            return try await callDeepSeek(messages: messages, context: context)
416|0935ee|        case .mistral:
417|048202|            return try await callMistral(messages: messages, context: context)
418|7b8ebd|        case .ollama:
419|20a226|            return try await callOllama(messages: messages, context: context)
420|5f3077|        }
421|27e597|    }

423|b90399|    // MARK: - OpenAI API
424|b4687f|    
425|c4fdfa|    private func callOpenAI(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {
426|bc2d67|        let url = URL(string: "\(AIProvider.openai.baseURL)/chat/completions")!
427|6007aa|        var request = URLRequest(url: url)
428|89eca9|        request.httpMethod = "POST"
429|7fd512|        request.setValue("Bearer \(openAIKey)", forHTTPHeaderField: "Authorization")
430|0b9fcc|        request.setValue("application/json", forHTTPHeaderField: "Content-Type")
431|d6ed84|        
432|84a07c|        var apiMessages: [[String: String]] = []
433|d6ed84|        
434|5740dd|        // Add system message with context

532|190d00|    private func callGoogle(messages: [ChatMessage], context: String?) async throws -> String {
533|dd3258|        let url = URL(string: "\(AIProvider.google.baseURL)/models/\(selectedModel.id):generateContent?key=\(googleKey)")!
534|6007aa|        var request = URLRequest(url: url)
535|89eca9|        request.httpMethod = "POST"
536|0b9fcc|        request.setValue("application/json", forHTTPHeaderField: "Content-Type")
537|d6ed84|        
538|2ae98d|        var parts: [[String: Any]] = []
539|d6ed84|        
540|288895|        // Add system context
541|fd71f7|        let systemPrompt = buildSystemPrompt(context: context)
542|e08e07|        parts.append(["text": "System: \(systemPrompt)"])
543|d6ed84|        
544|c1c8d4|        // Add messages
545|0c7100|        for msg in messages {
546|989b77|            let role = msg.role == .assistant ? "Model" : "User"
547|35f120|            parts.append(["text": "\(role): \(msg.content)"])
548|5f3077|        }
549|d6ed84|        
550|825e3e|        let body: [String: Any] = [
551|6251fc|            "contents": [
552|f76f20|                ["parts": parts]
553|97e7d5|            ],
554|0eaa6f|            "generationConfig": [
555|80d7f4|                "maxOutputTokens": 4096,
556|e772de|                "temperature": 0.7
557|324820|            ]
558|220505|        ]
559|d6ed84|        
560|bae13e|        request.httpBody = try JSONSerialization.data(withJSONObject: body)
561|d6ed84|        
562|57e527|        let (data, response) = try await URLSession.shared.data(for: request)
563|d6ed84|        
564|2748ab|        guard let httpResponse = response as? HTTPURLResponse else {
565|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
566|5f3077|        }
567|d6ed84|        
568|42034c|        if httpResponse.statusCode != 200 {
569|a214f5|            if let errorJson = try? JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any],
570|3cebbe|               let error = errorJson["error"] as? [String: Any],
571|be8727|               let message = error["message"] as? String {
572|f87f3a|                throw AIError.apiError(message)
573|a7dc16|            }
574|6baa43|            throw AIError.httpError(httpResponse.statusCode)
575|5f3077|        }
576|d6ed84|        
577|c94159|        let json = try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: data) as? [String: Any]
578|12af8b|        guard let candidates = json?["candidates"] as? [[String: Any]],
579|977b10|              let firstCandidate = candidates.first,
580|0ff2f5|              let content = firstCandidate["content"] as? [String: Any],

583|a6eafc|              let text = firstPart["text"] as? String else {
584|aa0282|            throw AIError.invalidResponse
585|5f3077|        }
586|d6ed84|

588|27e597|    }

933|791eb5|        var blocks: [CodeBlock] = []
934|0f2b2b|        let pattern = "```(\\w*)\\n([\\s\\S]*?)```"
935|d6ed84|        
936|cbccc8|        guard let regex = try? NSRegularExpression(pattern: pattern) else {
937|f7ed63|            return blocks
938|5f3077|        }

940|10d615|        let range = NSRange(text.startIndex..., in: text)
941|b29406|        let matches = regex.matches(in: text, range: range)
942|d6ed84|        
943|847e6d|        for match in matches {
944|b137ab|            if let langRange = Range(match.range(at: 1), in: text),
945|f66f31|               let codeRange = Range(match.range(at: 2), in: text) {
946|dfd4cc|                let language = String(text[langRange])
947|894c52|                let code = String(text[codeRange]).trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
948|9e5c94|                blocks.append(CodeBlock(language: language.isEmpty ? "text" : language, code: code))
949|a7dc16|            }
950|5f3077|        }
951|d6ed84|        
952|db7106|        return blocks
953|27e597|    }

412|e883ab|            let filePath = repoURL.appendingPathComponent(file)
413|7528cd|            try? FileManager.default.removeItem(at: filePath)
414|5f3077|        }
415|d6ed84|

417|27e597|    }

195|46f2b0|    func save(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {
196|518562|        var config = connection
197|33d6e7|        config.lastUsed = Date()
198|d6ed84|        
199|b12566|        if let index = savedConnections.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == config.id }) {
200|ca9b5c|            savedConnections[index] = config
201|b31999|        } else {
202|979f69|            savedConnections.append(config)
203|5f3077|        }
204|d6ed84|        
205|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
206|27e597|    }
207|b4687f|    
208|eea006|    func delete(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {

210|2d7bb4|        persistConnections()
211|27e597|    }
212|b4687f|    
213|c2f169|    func updateLastUsed(_ connection: SSHConnectionConfig) {

215|85969b|            savedConnections[index].lastUsed = Date()
216|da901b|            persistConnections()
217|5f3077|        }
218|27e597|    }
219|b4687f|    
220|ae0029|    private func loadConnections() {
221|e4c350|        guard let data = userDefaults.data(forKey: storageKey),
222|f8ff24|              let connections = try? JSONDecoder().decode([SSHConnectionConfig].self, from: data) else {
223|bef5d6|            return
224|5f3077|        }
225|a65f6e|        savedConnections = connections.sorted { ($0.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) > ($1.lastUsed ?? .distantPast) }
226|27e597|    }
227|b4687f|    
228|a3fceb|    private func persistConnections() {
229|7e12a8|        guard let data = try? JSONEncoder().encode(savedConnections) else { return }
230|ad5d30|        userDefaults.set(data, forKey: storageKey)
231|27e597|    }

19|c841df|    ///   - url: The file URL
20|6a8a9f|    ///   - content: The file content
21|a646b8|    ///   - fileName: The file name
22|c4dda7|    func indexFile(url: URL, content: String, fileName: String) {

24|d6ed84|        
25|795554|        // Basic attributes
26|b52257|        attributeSet.title = fileName

29|d6ed84|

36|d6ed84|        
37|2851f6|        // File metadata

39|1edb5f|        attributeSet.keywords = [fileName, fileExtension, "code", "editor"]
40|d6ed84|        
41|049cab|        // Determine content type based on extension
42|64a59e|        if let utType = UTType(filenameExtension: fileExtension) {

44|5f3077|        }

53|0b7aa7|        attributeSet.addedDate = Date()
54|d6ed84|

56|f0b8b3|        let uniqueIdentifier = url.path

59|c76664|            domainIdentifier: domainIdentifier,
60|9e98a4|            attributeSet: attributeSet
61|3143a4|        )

70|f5a6eb|            } else {

72|a7dc16|            }
73|5f3077|        }
74|27e597|    }

227|196f77|    /// VS Code `settings.json` can contain JSON with comments (JSONC). This strips
228|11a55b|    /// both `//` line comments and `/* ... */` block comments.
229|fb989d|    private static func stripJSONComments(_ input: String) -> String {
230|5749dc|        let blockPattern = "/\\*[^*]*\\*+(?:[^/*][^*]*\\*+)*/"
231|e0e74b|        let linePattern = "(?m)//.*$"
232|adc83b|
233|aec1b9|        let withoutBlocks = input.replacingOccurrences(of: blockPattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
234|1e4b82|        let withoutLines = withoutBlocks.replacingOccurrences(of: linePattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
235|2c31a3|        return withoutLines
236|27e597|    }

175|027474|// MARK: - Snippet Expansion
176|adc83b|
177|ffaefa|extension SnippetsManager {
178|a686f9|    /// Expands a snippet body and returns:
179|c54008|    /// - text: body with $1/$2... placeholders removed
180|ddc512|    /// - cursorOffset: position of $1 if present, else end of expanded text
181|30e1d8|    func expand(_ snippet: Snippet) -> (text: String, cursorOffset: Int) {
182|8d4784|        let body = snippet.body
183|adc83b|
184|6fa346|        var output = ""
185|dc4dbb|        var i = body.startIndex
186|f91403|        var placeholderOffsets: [Int: Int] = [:]
187|adc83b|
188|ee9951|        while i < body.endIndex {
189|6a78bd|            let ch = body[i]
190|7d24e6|            if ch == "$" {
191|dbcb8c|                var j = body.index(after: i)
192|993846|                var digits = ""
193|f76007|                while j < body.endIndex, body[j].isNumber {
194|c59af6|                    digits.append(body[j])
195|f350a6|                    j = body.index(after: j)
196|4e2d32|                }
197|adc83b|
198|e6f600|                if !digits.isEmpty, let n = Int(digits) {
199|f67692|                    if placeholderOffsets[n] == nil {
200|173495|                        placeholderOffsets[n] = output.count
201|c9717a|                    }
202|5d22b9|                    i = j
203|f41bef|                    continue
204|4e2d32|                }
205|a7dc16|            }
206|adc83b|
207|87962f|            output.append(ch)
208|e6010d|            i = body.index(after: i)
209|5f3077|        }
210|adc83b|
211|b2860b|        let cursorOffset = placeholderOffsets[1] ?? output.count
212|e982be|        return (output, cursorOffset)
213|27e597|    }

99|27e597|    }

177|5a8596|    /// Replaces all occurrences in the chosen scope.

181|205058|              let regex = buildRegex()

201|8c8340|                    withTemplate: replaceQuery
202|6f642e|                )

206|4e2d32|                }
207|a7dc16|            }
208|adc83b|

260|4e4994|    private func executeSearch() -> [SearchResult] {
261|808213|        guard let core = editorCore else { return [] }
262|06469e|        guard let regex = buildRegex() else { return [] }
263|adc83b|
264|b128e6|        struct Target {
265|d0d64f|            let url: URL?
266|649854|            let filePath: String

268|6ffdc2|            let content: String
269|5f3077|        }
270|adc83b|
271|422382|        let targets: [Target] = {
272|450a38|            switch searchScope {
273|08df20|            case .currentFile:
274|c935e6|                guard let tab = core.activeTab else { return [] }
275|666545|                let path = tab.url?.path ?? tab.fileName
276|57a63d|                return [Target(url: tab.url, filePath: path, fileName: tab.fileName, content: tab.content)]
277|adc83b|
278|231fff|            case .openFiles:
279|09a4e8|                return core.tabs.map { tab in

287|c4e083|                return urls.compactMap { url in
288|e86233|                    guard let content = try? String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8) else { return nil }
289|3223da|                    return Target(url: url, filePath: url.path, fileName: url.lastPathComponent, content: content)
290|4e2d32|                }
291|a7dc16|            }
292|41cc2d|        }()
293|adc83b|
294|ede8fe|        var results: [SearchResult] = []
295|87d422|        results.reserveCapacity(64)
296|adc83b|
297|7e02cf|        for target in targets {
298|e64b6f|            let text = target.content
299|922eef|            let nsText = text as NSString
300|adc83b|
301|a53603|            let searchRange: NSRange

303|e6cc02|               searchScope == .currentFile,
304|9b8ef5|               let selection = core.currentSelectionRange {
305|92f918|                searchRange = selection

308|a7dc16|            }
309|adc83b|
310|5842db|            let matches = regex.matches(in: text, options: [], range: searchRange)
311|7c58fe|            for match in matches {
312|ed8ef0|                let r = match.range
313|30dcc2|                guard let swiftRange = Range(r, in: text) else { continue }
314|adc83b|
315|9f4e6b|                // 1-based line number
316|854f7d|                let prefix = nsText.substring(to: min(r.location, nsText.length))
317|caf675|                let lineNumber = prefix.components(separatedBy: "\n").count
318|adc83b|
319|7f7e0b|                // Full line content
320|bab0af|                let lineRange = nsText.lineRange(for: r)

152|b724e3|    /// Insert text at all cursor positions
153|f215f3|    func insertText(_ text: String, in fullText: inout String) {
154|7af105|        // Process from start -> end while tracking how prior edits shift later cursor positions.
155|4dfc73|        let sortedCursors = cursors.sorted { $0.position < $1.position }
156|b4bd74|        var delta = 0
157|adc83b|
158|7e0829|        for cursor in sortedCursors {
159|6f5089|            guard let cursorIndex = cursors.firstIndex(where: { $0.id == cursor.id }) else { continue }
160|adc83b|
161|94aef6|            if let selectionRange = cursor.selectionRange {
162|240234|                let effectiveLocation = selectionRange.location + delta
163|33054a|                let effectiveRange = NSRange(location: effectiveLocation, length: selectionRange.length)
164|adc83b|
165|6c5a92|                guard let swiftRange = Range(effectiveRange, in: fullText) else { continue }
166|adc83b|
167|5e54f3|                fullText.replaceSubrange(swiftRange, with: text)
168|adc83b|
169|9ad989|                // Cursor ends after inserted text; selection cleared.
170|1cc5b7|                cursors[cursorIndex].position = effectiveLocation + text.count
171|c0748c|                cursors[cursorIndex].anchor = nil
172|adc83b|
173|27a6d2|                delta += (text.count - selectionRange.length)
174|f5a6eb|            } else {
175|2a24c0|                let effectivePosition = cursor.position + delta
176|4ce229|                let clamped = min(max(0, effectivePosition), fullText.count)
177|660e91|                let stringIndex = fullText.index(fullText.startIndex, offsetBy: clamped)
178|adc83b|
179|0958ea|                fullText.insert(contentsOf: text, at: stringIndex)
180|adc83b|
181|9b2357|                cursors[cursorIndex].position = clamped + text.count
182|1198fc|                delta += text.count
183|a7dc16|            }
184|5f3077|        }
185|adc83b|
186|4120e8|        // Keep state sane if multiple edits collapse cursors onto the same location.
187|55724c|        removeDuplicateCursors()
188|27e597|    }
189|b4687f|

193|b4bd74|        var delta = 0
194|adc83b|

250|63c94d|    func findAllOccurrences(of searchString: String, caseSensitive: Bool = true) -> [NSRange] {
251|35cdd0|        var ranges: [NSRange] = []
252|78712f|        var searchRange = startIndex..<endIndex
253|e443de|        let options: String.CompareOptions = caseSensitive ? [] : .caseInsensitive
254|d6ed84|

259|5f3077|        }

262|27e597|    }

265|33836c|    func findNextOccurrence(of searchString: String, after position: Int, caseSensitive: Bool = true) -> NSRange? {
266|e6a5fe|        guard position < count else { return nil }
267|0c49ab|        let startIdx = index(startIndex, offsetBy: position)
268|e443de|        let options: String.CompareOptions = caseSensitive ? [] : .caseInsensitive
269|d6ed84|

271|a22c8b|        if let range = self.range(of: searchString, options: options, range: startIdx..<endIndex) {
272|8406dc|            return NSRange(range, in: self)
273|5f3077|        }
274|d6ed84|

50|b298bb|    // Helper for Hex Colors
51|8792bd|    static func hex(_ hex: String) -> Color {
52|a7cf95|        var hexSanitized = hex.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines)
53|47dd68|        hexSanitized = hexSanitized.replacingOccurrences(of: "#", with: "")
54|d6ed84|        
55|d3af08|        var rgb: UInt64 = 0
56|f1bde0|        Scanner(string: hexSanitized).scanHexInt64(&rgb)
57|d6ed84|        
58|61c152|        let r = Double((rgb & 0xFF0000) >> 16) / 255.0
59|c6183b|        let g = Double((rgb & 0x00FF00) >> 8) / 255.0
60|3cf70f|        let b = Double(rgb & 0x0000FF) / 255.0
61|d6ed84|        
62|8616b6|        return Color(red: r, green: g, blue: b)
63|27e597|    }

121|288471|        lastErrorMessage = nil
122|741d33|        workspaceSettings = .empty
123|adc83b|
124|de1de1|        guard let root = workspaceRootURL else { return }
125|adc83b|
126|29c204|        let settingsURL = root
127|f52c63|            .appendingPathComponent(".vscode", isDirectory: true)
128|ac5c20|            .appendingPathComponent("settings.json", isDirectory: false)
129|adc83b|
130|4da690|        do {
131|fcc4aa|            let data = try Data(contentsOf: settingsURL)
132|123a84|            let raw = String(decoding: data, as: UTF8.self)
133|9e9702|            let stripped = Self.stripJSONComments(raw)
134|537543|            let obj = try JSONSerialization.jsonObject(with: Data(stripped.utf8), options: [])
135|adc83b|
136|6ffd29|            guard let dict = obj as? [String: Any] else {
137|af3e64|                lastErrorMessage = "Couldn’t parse .vscode/settings.json"
138|53ab34|                return
139|a7dc16|            }
140|adc83b|
141|0e7035|            workspaceSettings = Self.parseWorkspaceSettings(from: dict)
142|853889|        } catch {

144|e71453|            // Only show an error if the file exists but couldn't be read.
145|f2176e|            if FileManager.default.fileExists(atPath: settingsURL.path) {
146|90691f|                lastErrorMessage = "Couldn’t load .vscode/settings.json"
147|a7dc16|            }
148|5f3077|        }
149|27e597|    }

162|bef5d6|            return

167|adc83b|

173|adc83b|

177|adc83b|

179|853889|        } catch {

182|27e597|    }

185|adc83b|
186|ad13c4|    private static func parseWorkspaceSettings(from dict: [String: Any]) -> WorkspaceSettings {
187|6e7c49|        func int(_ key: String) -> Int? {
188|2a8834|            dict[key] as? Int
189|5f3077|        }
190|6abde4|        func bool(_ key: String) -> Bool? {
191|ad025c|            dict[key] as? Bool
192|5f3077|        }
193|9ee76d|        func string(_ key: String) -> String? {
194|bef963|            dict[key] as? String
195|5f3077|        }
196|5d9d58|        func double(_ key: String) -> Double? {
197|e3c63f|            if let d = dict[key] as? Double { return d }
198|af9729|            if let i = dict[key] as? Int { return Double(i) }
199|1c8557|            return nil
200|5f3077|        }
201|adc83b|
202|260924|        return WorkspaceSettings(
203|c5ac08|            tabSize: int("editor.tabSize"),
204|dbd09f|            insertSpaces: bool("editor.insertSpaces"),
205|90f950|            formatOnSave: bool("editor.formatOnSave"),
206|8561bc|            theme: string("workbench.colorTheme"),
207|1accf7|            fontFamily: string("editor.fontFamily"),
208|335677|            fontSize: double("editor.fontSize")
209|3143a4|        )
210|27e597|    }

213|4bd403|        var dict: [String: Any] = [:]
214|adc83b|
215|5c5c54|        if let tabSize = settings.tabSize { dict["editor.tabSize"] = tabSize }
216|a7ff32|        if let insertSpaces = settings.insertSpaces { dict["editor.insertSpaces"] = insertSpaces }
217|8cb06f|        if let formatOnSave = settings.formatOnSave { dict["editor.formatOnSave"] = formatOnSave }
218|cddc56|        if let theme = settings.theme, !theme.isEmpty { dict["workbench.colorTheme"] = theme }
219|cd41fb|        if let fontFamily = settings.fontFamily, !fontFamily.isEmpty { dict["editor.fontFamily"] = fontFamily }
220|49f99f|        if let fontSize = settings.fontSize { dict["editor.fontSize"] = fontSize }
221|adc83b|
222|7849e9|        return dict
223|27e597|    }

225|ae92ad|    // MARK: - JSONC helpers
226|adc83b|
227|196f77|    /// VS Code `settings.json` can contain JSON with comments (JSONC). This strips
228|11a55b|    /// both `//` line comments and `/* ... */` block comments.
229|fb989d|    private static func stripJSONComments(_ input: String) -> String {
230|5749dc|        let blockPattern = "/\\*[^*]*\\*+(?:[^/*][^*]*\\*+)*/"
231|e0e74b|        let linePattern = "(?m)//.*$"
232|adc83b|
233|aec1b9|        let withoutBlocks = input.replacingOccurrences(of: blockPattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
234|1e4b82|        let withoutLines = withoutBlocks.replacingOccurrences(of: linePattern, with: "", options: .regularExpression)
235|2c31a3|        return withoutLines
236|27e597|    }

Scope I was able to verify:
- Read **all files in `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Models/`** (8 files).
- Attempted to locate `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Managers/` via `list_dir`; it **does not exist** (tool returned “Directory … not found”). No other `Managers/` directory was found via directory listing.
- To answer “what data persists”, I additionally read several persistence-relevant “manager” classes located under **`VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Services/`**: `SettingsManager.swift`, `RecentFileManager.swift`, `WorkspaceManager.swift`, `WindowStateManager.swift`.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## 1) Models folder: real implementations vs stubs

### `Models/EditorState.swift` (real data model; no persistence)
- Pure state structs/enums: `EditorState`, `CursorPosition (Codable)`, `TextSelection (Codable)`, `SplitViewConfiguration (Codable)` with helper methods.
- No disk/UserDefaults interaction anywhere in file.
Evidence:
- Definitions and helpers are concrete (e.g., folding + selection helpers) `EditorState.toggleFolding` etc. (lines 12-117).
- Cursor + selection are Codable but not persisted here (lines 122-248).
- SplitViewConfiguration Codable w/ computed props (lines 252-296).

**Stub/fake?** No explicit stub. It’s an in-memory state container only (no persistence layer attached).

---

### `Models/FileItem.swift` (real UI model; no persistence)
- Real struct used to represent filesystem nodes, provides icon/color helpers.
Evidence:
- `struct FileItem ...` plus computed properties `fileExtension`, `icon`, `iconColor` and helper switch on extension (lines 4-81).

**Persists?** No.

---

### `Models/FileItemUTType.swift` (tiny implementation; no persistence)
- Extends `UTType` with a custom type identifier.
Evidence:
- `extension UTType { static let fileItem ... }` (lines 6-13).

**Note (possible integration/compile issue, not a stub):**
- File contains no `import UniformTypeIdentifiers`; it relies on `UTType` being in scope elsewhere. (entire file is lines 2-15)

---

### `Models/FindViewModel.swift` (real implementation; mixed in-memory + on-disk read/write via EditorCore)
- Fully implemented find/replace logic with debounce, scopes (current/open/workspace), regex options, and replace operations.
Evidence:
- Debounced search pipeline: `performSearch()` schedules `executeSearch()` (lines 71-99).
- Workspace search reads files from disk: `String(contentsOf: url, encoding: .utf8)` (lines 284-290).
- Workspace replace writes to disk: `try? replaced.write(to: url, atomically: true, encoding: .utf8)` (lines 232-241).
- Also includes UI Views (`FindReplaceView`, `SearchResultsListView`) in same file (lines 367-511).

**Stub/fake?** Not a stub; actual behavior implemented. “Persisted data” here is only when replacing workspace files (writes to actual file URLs).

---

### `Models/MultiCursor.swift` (real implementation; no persistence)
- Real multi-cursor logic: cursor list, insertion/deletion across multiple cursors, deduping.
Evidence:
- `MultiCursorState.insertText` and `deleteBackward` mutate text and cursor positions (lines 152-223).
- Includes occurrence finding helpers on `String` (lines 248-282).

**Stub/fake?**
- `adjustCursorPositions(afterInsertion:)` is a no-op with comment “Already handled…” (lines 225-227). This is the closest thing to a “stub”, but it’s not used and the real logic is elsewhere.

---

### `Models/Tab.swift` (real model; no persistence by itself)
- Real tab model with metadata, language detection, computed props, Codable conformance.
Evidence:
- `struct Tab ... Codable` with fields `fileName`, `content`, `url`, `isUnsaved`, etc. (lines 13-42).
- Language auto-detection in initializer (lines 76-82).
- `CodeLanguage` enum supports extension->language mapping (lines 148-191).

**Persists?** Not here. It’s Codable, but no code in this file encodes/decodes or writes it anywhere.

---

### `Models/Theme.swift` (real static theme catalog; no persistence)
- Large set of hardcoded themes and `Theme.allThemes`.
Evidence:
- Theme definition + `hex` helper (lines 3-63).
- `static let allThemes: [Theme] = [...]` (lines 865-886).

**Persists?** No; these are constants.

---

### `Models/ThemeManager.swift` (real persistence of selected theme via UserDefaults/AppStorage)
- Stores a `selectedThemeId` and derives `currentTheme` from `Theme.allThemes`.
Evidence:
- `@AppStorage("selectedThemeId") var selectedThemeId ...` (line 5)
- Reads `UserDefaults.standard.string(forKey: "selectedThemeId")` in `init()` (line 14)
- Writes selection back via `self.selectedThemeId = themeId` (line 23)

**Stub/fake?** Not a stub: it actually persists to user defaults via `@AppStorage`.
**Potential issue (not a stub, but noteworthy):**
- File only `import Combine` (line 2) but uses `@AppStorage`, `withAnimation`, and `Color` in `color(for:)` (lines 5, 20, 63-75). This suggests it likely needs `import SwiftUI` to compile.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## 2) “Managers/” directory status
- `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Managers/` does **not exist** (list_dir error: directory not found). I can’t read “ALL files” in a directory that isn’t present.

However, there are many “manager” classes under `VSCodeiPadOS/VSCodeiPadOS/Services/` (confirmed by directory listing), so the intended target may have been that folder.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## 3) What data actually persists? What’s fake?

### Persists (verified in code)
1) **Selected theme**
- Persisted key: `selectedThemeId` in UserDefaults/AppStorage.
Evidence: `Models/ThemeManager.swift` line 5 (`@AppStorage("selectedThemeId")`) and lines 14-16 (read defaults) + line 23 (write).

2) **Editor/global settings**
- Persisted keys in UserDefaults via `@AppStorage`:
  - `fontSize`, `fontFamily`, `tabSize`, `wordWrap`, `autoSave` (`autoSaveRaw`), `minimapEnabled`
Evidence: `Services/SettingsManager.swift` lines 11-34 (all `@AppStorage(...)`).

3) **Recent files list**
- Persisted key: `recentFileURLs` (array of URL strings) in UserDefaults.
Evidence: `Services/RecentFileManager.swift`:
  - `defaultsKey = "recentFileURLs"` (line 8)
  - save: `UserDefaults.standard.set(urlStrings, forKey: defaultsKey)` (line 31)
  - load: `UserDefaults.standard.stringArray(forKey: defaultsKey)` (line 35)

4) **Workspace (per-project) settings**
- Persisted on disk at: `<workspaceRoot>/.vscode/settings.json`
Evidence: `Services/WorkspaceManager.swift`:
  - load reads Data from `.vscode/settings.json` (lines 126-134)
  - save creates `.vscode/` dir and writes settings.json atomically (lines 165-179)

5) **Multi-window state**
- Persisted in UserDefaults as JSON-encoded `[UUID: WindowState]` under key `com.vscode-ipados.windowStates`.
Evidence: `Services/WindowStateManager.swift`:
  - `statesKey` (line 95)
  - load: `userDefaults.data(forKey:)` + `JSONDecoder().decode` (lines 104-111)
  - save: `JSONEncoder().encode(windowStates)` then `userDefaults.set(data, forKey:)` (lines 113-117)

6) **Find/Replace “workspace replace” modifies real files**
- Not “app state persistence”, but it writes changes to actual workspace files.
Evidence: `Models/FindViewModel.swift` line 240 (`try? replaced.write(to: url, ...)`).

### Does NOT persist (in the reviewed Models)
- `EditorState`, `CursorPosition`, `TextSelection`, `SplitViewConfiguration` are in-memory only; Codable exists but unused for storage in this file (EditorState.swift lines 12-296).
- `Tab` is Codable but there is no encoding/writing logic in `Tab.swift` (lines 13-143). So tab/session persistence is not implemented here.
- `MultiCursorState` is fully functional but purely in-memory (`MultiCursor.swift` lines 58-243).
- `FileItem` is a UI model only (`FileItem.swift` lines 4-81).
- `Theme` is a static catalog only (`Theme.swift` lines 3-886).

### “Fake” / misleading signals
- The main “looks persistent but isn’t” case in Models is **`Tab: Codable`**: it suggests potential session persistence, but there is no persistence implementation in `Models/Tab.swift` itself (lines 13-143). Any real persistence would have to be elsewhere.

-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## 4) Quick classification table (Models)

- `EditorState.swift`: real implementation (in-memory state), no persistence.
- `FileItem.swift`: real implementation (UI/fs node model), no persistence.
- `FileItemUTType.swift`: real implementation (UTType definition), no persistence.
- `FindViewModel.swift`: real implementation; can read/write workspace files during replace.
- `MultiCursor.swift`: real implementation; one unused no-op helper.
- `Tab.swift`: real model; Codable but no persistence here.
- `Theme.swift`: real static data; no persistence.
- `ThemeManager.swift`: real persistence of selected theme via AppStorage/UserDefaults.
